font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许那：带离原来监区，暂不知去向<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">因疫情期间发布一些国<span lang="EN-US">/</span>内疫情照片，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在家中被警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被从北京市东城区看守所转至天河监狱调遣处，约于同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被转入北京女子监狱三分监区十班，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年初被突然带离三分监区，不知去向。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/8202432.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/8202432.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许那：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，当年天安门广场上的绝食学生中，有一位名叫许那（又名许娜），是北京广播学院（现中国传媒大学）的学生。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年前，她曾和同学高举“新闻自由，言论自由”的横幅，满怀希望地走在北京街头游行的人群中。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年后，许那仍在北京，却已在东城区看守所被刑事羁押了一年多时间。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，许那和于宙在参加一场同道聚会后双双被拘留四十多天。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，许那因为外地来京的法轮功朋友提供住宿而再次被捕，后被判五年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年初，随着奥运会的临近，各地异议人士遭到抓捕，包括法轮功修炼者。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上，于宙、许那在演唱会结束后开车回家的路上，被警方拦住搜查。警察在其车中搜出一本法轮功书籍，将夫妇二人带到通州拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天后正值除夕，体格健壮的于宙突然离奇死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁。当局声称于宙死于绝食或糖尿病。悲痛欲绝的许那被判处三年有期徒刑。于宙的真实死因至今成谜。于宙、许那的案件见于国际特赦<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月向联合国普遍定期审议递交的报告、美国“国会及行政当局中国委员会”的分析报告、美国国际宗教自由委员会<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度报告。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，许那第三次被捕。当天<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括许那在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。许那等人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，许那被北京当局宣判，获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬已被转监到北京女子监狱服刑。后遭带离，不知去向。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李建新：<a name="_Hlk162481558">经家属交涉，重回老弱病残监区<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></a></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162481558;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李建新</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原来是广东省惠州著名的维权人士，被人称为“惠阳区伯”。因为举报村官贪腐、官商勾结等违法行径，特别是实名举报原惠州市副市长黄锦辉，李建新被人报复殴打、泼硫酸毁容，右眼失明，达到<span lang="EN-US">4</span>级伤残。后<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年又被当局设套构陷入罪，被广东省惠州市惠东县法院强判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，惠州市中院二审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年，李建新从广东省惠东县看守所转到广州从化监狱第十二监区二分区服刑，该分区是老、弱、病、残服刑人员分监区，基本没有强迫劳动任务。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月间，从化监狱把李建新从第十二监区二分区调到第六监区，该监区要参加高强度的定额强迫劳动，严重残疾的李建新根本无法胜任，而监狱又非法规定不能完成生产任务的服刑人员下班后要接受两小时的变相体罚，还要被扣分，影响减刑。经家属要求，李建新才重回到第十二监区二分区。截止目前，李建新只有两次减刑，共计减刑一年刑期；暂不考虑后续减刑，刑期截止到<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/11202436.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/11202436.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李建新：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省惠州市人，人称“惠州区伯”，实名举报人，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。因长期网上实名举报广东惠州官员的贪腐行为，而引起媒体关注和社会热议；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因其举报惠州市副市长黄锦辉，随遭遇报复性砍伤并被泼硫酸，导致其一只眼睛失明、手脚被砍断，留下终身残疾；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，因其继续维权，坚持网络实名举报，遂被惠州市惠城区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被惠阳区检察院以涉嫌“敲诈勒索”和“非法占用耕地”二罪名正式批捕，并被关押于惠东县看守所，指控其索要他人<span lang="EN-US">350</span>万元以换取两则网上删除的信息，因此属于违反敲诈勒索罪；而一些知情网友则称，其之所以被当局刑拘和起诉，是因为他长期举报惠州贪官所受到的构陷与报复；其案后来经惠州市惠阳区检察院退回补充侦查二次、延长审查起诉期限二次，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被起诉于惠州市惠阳区法院，但该法院又于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日发出通知书，告知经惠州市中级法院决定该案由惠东县法院管辖，随后其案再被移交到惠州市惠东县检察院审查起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其被广东省惠州市惠东县法院一审，去掉“非法占用耕地罪”，以“敲诈勒索罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，原刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。截止目前，李建新只有两次减刑，共计减刑一年刑期；暂不考虑后续减刑，刑期截止到<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。目前在广州从化监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王建辉：遭酷刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年的黑龙江大庆市法轮功学员<a name="_Hlk162481971">王建辉</a>女士在黑龙江省女子监狱遭惨无人道的酷刑折磨。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span _Hlk162566522;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/5_6.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江大庆市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，大庆油田总医院职工，家住大庆市萨尔图区。在中共对法轮功持续至今二十多年的迫害中，王建辉屡遭中共人员绑架、抄家、关押、劳教、判刑等迫害：<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押在黑龙江省女子戒毒劳教所：<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被大庆市萨尔图区铁人公安分局便衣警察抓捕，关押在大庆市第二看守所，遭构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年并罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，王建辉被转监到黑龙江省女子监狱八监区。王建辉在八监区遭受监狱指使的包夹犯人惨无人道的酷刑折磨，甚至将厕所拖布塞其嘴、反复碾踩其十趾。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王刚：遭严管，不准律师家人会见<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2024</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，代理律师及家人要求会见王刚，邢台监狱称：因为王刚不服从监管规定，散布不当言论，现在严管期不允许律师或者家属会见。严管为期三个月，三个月后家属和律师才可以会见。此次虽没有见到王刚，但了解到王刚身体还行，王刚脸上的带状疱疹还在抹药。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span _Hlk162566522;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/26_28.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王刚：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1958</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，河北省人，原河北工程大学临床医学院副教授，人类党网站（或人类党论坛）作者<span lang="EN-US">, </span>笔名“诺亚方舟”，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。十几年前，曾因发表多篇评论时政及反思文革的文章，而被其任职大学所在地河北省邯郸市当局视为重点监控对像；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，又因质疑中共享人制度及专制腐败现像等，发表《致中共中央的公开信》，呼吁政治改革，而被邯郸市丛台区警方贴身监控；后因其不惧危险，仍旧经常在微信上发表批评政府的文章，而曾被邯郸市警方处治安拘留<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次（第一次拘留<span lang="EN-US">19</span>天，第二次拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天），被喝茶<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多次；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因再次呼吁中共反腐和政改等，后又于同年创立“上海百姓维权”与“中国百姓维权”等微信群，表明中共绝不会走民主宪政之路，故而呼吁“民众移民”，但此言行被警方获悉，遂立遭丛台区联西派出所警方的野蛮执法，并派专人以“科研助手”名义对其进行贴身监视；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，“六四”来临前夕，其频遭当地警方约谈和做笔录，并被威胁称，若其尽快退出微信群，且不再在网上发表违规言论，就不对其翻旧账，但若继续发声，不仅会被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10-15</span>天，更会将其以前的案子推翻，再以“颠覆国家政权罪”论处；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其突遭警方立案侦查，并由公安部统一部署，在全国五六个省份（如闽、粤、湘和海南等省） 对其展开调查；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被邯郸市丛台区丛西派出所警方以约谈之名诱骗至派出所后失联，至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉，其已被邯郸市丛台区警方正式刑事拘留，罪名是涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权。被羁押于邯郸市第一看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日由邯郸市公安局移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底宣判，王刚被以煽动颠覆国家政权罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。判刑后已被转监至河北邢台监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐光：不予律师会见，身体堪忧<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">浙江杭州民主党人、八九学生领袖徐光先是在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被刑事拘留的，至今已被羁押超过<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，其在狱中身体堪忧。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号，徐光的辩护律师吴有水近日到看守所去会见徐光，看守所未予安排会见，理由是徐光本人提出不见律师，吴律师未见到徐光本人，不知是否徐光本人真实意愿。在吴有水律师安排会见徐光之前，徐光的另一位律师纪中久也到看守所会见徐光，看守所接到律师会见手续后，等待一阵子回复说徐光身体不佳，没能安排会见。徐光姐姐接到此消息后，为徐光身体担心。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/19.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/19.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐光：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生于浙江省富阳市，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年毕业于杭州大学生物系，大学期间曾参与<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年及<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年学生爱国民主运动，“八九学运”杭州大学学运领袖，中国民主党浙江委员会核心成员，于<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月在家乡富阳市环保局环境监测站工作的徐光组建了“中国民主党浙江省富阳市筹委会”，是中国民主党第一个县级组织。撰写了《抓不完的中国民主党》等文章，并起草《中国民主党富阳市筹备委员会成立公开宣言》，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被杭州市抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>被逮捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日徐光被以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；出狱后的徐光仍坚守信念，抨击时弊。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日因为在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>上参加中国民主党话题的闲聊，被浙江当局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被正式逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获释，期间从未获准律师会见。后获释。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因“六四”将近，徐光收到居住区西湖区公局分局玉泉派出所的传唤单，徐光未予理睬。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，徐光在所居东山弄小区采购，途经辖区的西湖区公安分局玉泉派出所附近，正遇上派出所民警，被带进派出所，告诫徐光“六四”将近，不要有什么涉“六四”的敏感言行，强行收走了他的手机。徐光<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日去玉泉派出所，带着写着“平反六四”的纸张，抗议公安对自己迫害。当日徐光被国保刑事拘留，被抄家，后被羁押。徐光从当日绝食抗议至今仍在绝食中，鼻饲灌注维持。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>时杭州国保第二次对徐光家搜查，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日正式逮捕徐光。徐光被控的罪名为涉嫌寻衅滋事。当局指控徐光“在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年期间，在微信，脸书，电报，油管发布视频，文章，散布损害国家形象，危害国家利益的虚假信息。指控徐光在网络上寻衅滋事。”徐光认为系当局构陷，徐光称：自己作为当年杭州六四学运的参予者，每年都公开纪念“八九六四”和举牌“勿忘六四”。当局为六四维稳需要，打压中国民主党人，在六四前抓捕自己。徐光坚决要求律师做无罪辩护。现徐光关押在杭州市西湖区分局看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">史庭福：被羁押在新疆阿克苏地区阿拉尔市看守所<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">南京公民、基督徒<a name="_Hlk162485338">史庭福</a>因帮助新疆阿克苏生产建设兵团果农维权，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被阿拉尔市城区公安局抓捕随即被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日史庭福被正式批捕。现被控涉嫌网络编造、传播虚假维权信息寻衅滋事，另有发现其有传播宣扬恐怖主义、极端主义的网络行为故而不准予律师会见。史庭福现<a name="_Hlk162485369">被羁押在新疆阿克苏地区阿拉尔市看守所</a>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/blog-post_49.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/blog-post_49.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">史庭福：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原是南京一位争取私权利的普通访民，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁。他是一位在恶劣的环境下一步步成长为热心的维权人士，具有令中共当局恐惧的公民意识，认同三民主义与普世价值观，更是属于街头行动派的一员。他曾在南京中山陵当众喊话到访的原国民党主席的洪秀柱，希望国民党坚守民主理念；也曾现场关注南京维权人士王健被构陷案；更在苏州“<span lang="EN-US">4.29</span>”祭奠林昭时被带走。多年来，除身体力行外，史庭福先生还在网络上声援郭飞雄，为困境中的人权律师发声，在自己经济条件非常困难情况下，还资助其他更困难的维权路上的同道。此前，史庭福<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因宣讲六四真相而被控“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕案<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在南京法庭判史庭福犯寻衅滋事罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，史庭福先生出狱。史庭福因帮助新疆阿克苏生产建设兵团果农维权于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被阿拉尔市城区公安局抓捕随即被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日史庭福被正式批捕。现被控涉嫌网络编造、传播虚假维权信息寻衅滋事，另有发现其有传播宣扬恐怖主义、极端主义的网络行为故而不准予律师会见。史庭福现被羁押在新疆阿克苏地区阿拉尔市看守所。据悉史庭福目前患有高血压、肺炎、哮喘病，身体一直不好，其被新疆警方跨省抓捕，境况令人担忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王春玲：不准探视<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年吉林市法轮功学员王春玲吉林省女子监狱中拒绝所谓“转化”，吉林省女子监狱不许家人探视。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span _Hlk162566522;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/4_15.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/4_15.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王春玲：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年生，家住吉林市龙潭区缸窑镇，因坚持修炼法轮功，多次被抓捕迫害。王春玲<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在发放法轮功资料时被吉林市新安派出所警察抓捕，关押在看守所，一直没有任何消息。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月朋友去看守所存东西才得知王春玲获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。王春玲已于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被转监到长春女子监狱，至今已五个月了。吉林省女子监狱以她不放弃信仰为由，一直不让王春玲的家人探视她。这令王春玲的家人非常担心她的健康及安全。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张晓东：一审开庭<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2022</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被抓捕的江西南昌公民<a name="_Hlk162501347">张晓东</a>已被羁押一年四个月了。其被起诉书指控涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，而证据全是其在微信群、朋友圈、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群里的所谓言论，是典型的因言获罪。今天（<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日）上午<span lang="EN-US">10:00</span>张晓东的寻衅滋事案在南昌市青山湖区法院审理，据悉张晓东坚信自己无罪。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/blog-post_95.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/blog-post_95.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张晓东：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西南昌人士，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日生。铁路部门停薪留职，下海经商多年，已退休。为人热情慷慨，好交友。每有朋友落难，包括本地公民朋友与律师落难，他都会奔走帮助。张晓东<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被当地警方抓捕，随后就遭刑事拘留。后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被批准逮捕。张晓东与‘江西九江四公民’案被捕人员均为好友。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被移送检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日开庭审理。目前张晓东现羁押在南昌市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙：二审开庭<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的著名人权捍卫者<a name="_Hlk162503029">季孝龙</a>案二审于今天下午在上海第一中级人民法院第六庭开庭。季孝龙的父亲季兴华到上海中院旁听了季孝龙的二审开庭，二审没有当庭宣判，季父强烈谴责法庭依然用伪证陷害自己的儿子。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/46_22.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，江苏省张家港市人，张家港市杨舍镇名都花苑居民，基督徒，维权公民，民主人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因宣传民主理念而被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由传唤，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，并在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写宣传语“大病治不起，习胖狂撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时毕！打倒共产党。还政于民，结束民众苦难。推翻习核心，拒走文革路”等字句，短时间内响应者众多，随于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被送到指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪由转正式逮捕，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被上海市浦东新区检察院起诉至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后送上海市白茅岭监狱七监区服刑；据悉，羁押期间，警方曾多次以让其“死亡”和用寒冷气温逼迫其认罪，致其身体健康虚弱且生病吐血；其家属曾送羽绒服和《圣经》书籍亦遭拒收；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刑满获释；同年上海封城，其为上海市民持续发声。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，再次被上海市梅园新村派出所警察从家中带走，后被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，又被浦东新检察院以同罪名正式批捕，后季孝龙于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被起诉。后已经开庭，未宣判。最终于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被一些寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前被羁押于浦东新区看守所（上海市浦东新区华益路<span lang="EN-US">351</span>号，邮政编码<span lang="EN-US">: 201210</span>）。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2024</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，陈家鸿的代理律师在广西玉林的北流市看守所会见了陈家鸿，陈家鸿目前精神状态不错。在会见中陈家鸿表达了自己无罪的意见。他认为自己在私人场合和老同学的对话内容不构成寻性滋事罪，不应该被追究刑事责任。对另一起伪造企业单位印章罪名，陈家鸿辩解认为这是自己的的单位，使用该单位的印章合理合法。他向承办法官提交了二十多份申请，希望法官能批准申请事项，以保证程序合法。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span _Hlk162566522;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/2024324.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><a name="_Hlk162504031"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈家鸿</span></b></a></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1966</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，广西壮族自治区北流县隆盛镇平坡村人，又名陈文胆，字数真，早年为广西北流县鸭壤小学教师，知名业余书法家、字画家，原南宁市百举鸣律师事务所执业律师，敏感案件代理人，中国人权律师团成员，人权律师，政治犯。自从成为“百举鸣律师事务所”（现已被当局取缔）中一名执业律师以来，因长期参与维权敏感案件，追求民主人权并为之积极发声，随屡遭中共当局严打逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因积极介入了震惊网络的“广西村民罗继标在看守所离奇死亡事件”，而遭广西警方的持枪围困；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，曾因同一事件，其介入维权行为被广西律师协会视为违规，从而被该律师协会给予“公开谴责行业处分的通报”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，又被南宁市司法局行政处罚停业半年；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其被北流县警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕、刑拘，其家被查抄；之后，其又被北流县检察院以同罪由予以批捕，并被指控因其反对官员腐败、呼吁建立民主宪政等带有政治倾向的公开言论、书法作品及行为艺术等涉及挑战现政权，尤其是其中一副书法作品，内含“成立暗杀突击队！清算邪恶官僚，加速民主进程”等激进敏感字眼，触犯了政府的相关法律条例，其行为属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案件被地方检察院移交至玉林巿中级法院起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，终被玉林市中级法院在其辩护律师未到场的情况下，一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日；此前被羁押于广西玉林市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底又遭当局刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被批捕。羁押在广西玉林的北流市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk162505153">何斌、徐彩虹夫妇</a>：已经开庭两次，仍未判决<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北襄阳维权人士何斌、徐彩虹夫妇自从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被警方从北京带回户籍居住地湖北襄樊关押后，至今羁押已达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初就已移送检察院，后获悉，何斌、徐彩虹“寻衅滋事”案目前已经开庭两次，但仍未判决。何斌、徐彩虹夫妇两人都是基督徒，早先因私有财产被侵占而维权多年，期间也因悼念六四或参与关注其他被侵权事件而受打压或关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/blog-post_26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/blog-post_26.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何斌：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1970</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年代出生，湖北省襄阳市人，基督徒，个体经营者，维权公民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，曾因何斌和妻子徐彩虹在当地创办了第一个实体店品牌“爱点”超市，并经努力经营使之快速成为当地同行业生意最火企业，遂冲闯了湖北省襄樊市（自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起更名为襄阳市）地方政府利益集团的奶酪，不仅频遭黑白两道的连手打击，而且曾因其二人长期在北京维权，利用网络参与围观声援维权律师、访民及民主异见人士等活动，而被多地警察驱赶、拘禁甚至被构陷入狱；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，曾因其及妻子控告李克强等中共最高领导人而遭报复性打压，被拘捕后欲判入狱，幸得其妻抱着与其同归于尽的决心为其呼吁和营救，才被当局在对其非法关押半年多后释放；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因其夫妻二人在京给美国飓风灾区捐款而被北京市朝阳区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”拘捕，后被北京朝阳区法院枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，并被送北京市朝阳看守所继关押；据悉，关押期间因遭非人道待遇而出监时暴瘦<span lang="EN-US">20</span>斤；自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，几乎每年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>敏感日期间，曾因参加或将要参加六四纪念活动，而被北京市不同区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”带走刑拘，并遭殴打受伤；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日因一宗租赁纠纷案件而与妻子在京长时间上访，遂被截访人员遣回原籍，并于次日再度被湖北省襄阳市樊城区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，又被樊城区警方转正式逮捕；后遭起诉，一直维开庭审理。目前何斌、徐彩虹都被羁押于襄阳市第二看守所（湖北省襄樊市樊城区王寨，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">441002</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">12/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk162505341"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廉长年、廉旭亮、付娟</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：案已到法院三人被均求刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西安丰盛教会的牧师、传道人廉长年、廉旭亮、付娟，自<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被控“诈骗罪”被羁押已超过<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，今年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底他们的案子已进入法院，起诉金额为<span lang="EN-US">39</span>万元，三人被检方均求刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<b>信息来源<span lang="EN-US">:</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/5_26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廉长年<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省人，基督徒，原河南“中华福音团契”（中国五大家庭教会之一）老一辈牧者，西安丰盛基督教教会创建人，主任牧师。上世纪<span lang="EN-US">90</span>年代廉长年牧师在西安市建立了丰盛基督教教会；但自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月中共新《宗教事务条例》正式生效实施起，全国各地基督教家庭教会纷纷遭遇空前严打和迫害，其所建西安丰盛教会亦遭严打和冲击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，自<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日始，其教会信徒突遭西安市灞桥区十里铺派出所警方大规模口头传唤和上门问讯，甚至有些人家被多次搜查，旨在胁迫信徒们作证，控告牧师诈骗和传播邪教，甚至要求信徒捏造有关教会奉献的虚假信息；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其及妻子、儿子、儿媳以及教会同工等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被当地派出所警方强行带走并被抄家，次日，其父子二人和教会财务同工付娟等人被西安市灞桥区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”指定居所监视居住；后遭刑事拘留、逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其教会被西安市民政局迅速发布通告取缔，理由是其与“中华福音总会”、“中华福音总会”西安区联会，“未经登记”就擅自以社会团体名义开展活动，故被认定为非法社会组织；其案虽已有多名维权律师介入，但其等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人曾被长期秘押，警方一直以当事人案情涉及危害国家安全为由拒绝律师会见。现案件已经到法院，检察院以诈骗罪对其求刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四、本期获悉狱中被迫害致死的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘殿元、李凤兰、李玉珍、费淑芹、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"></span><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘殿元<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省朝阳市凌源市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1938</span>年生。一九九五年，刘殿元开始修炼法轮功，中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年迫害法轮功后，刘殿元坚持真、善、忍信仰，遭到残酷迫害，多次被抓捕、关押，被非法劳教、判刑。因坚持法轮功信仰，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年时年<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁高龄的刘殿元先生被朝阳市建平县法院法判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年半。最终，他没能熬到出狱的那一天，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日（大年初一）在沈阳第一监狱被迫害致死，终年<span lang="EN-US">87</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，刘殿元家属接到沈阳第一监狱电话，称刘殿元老人于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日去世。据悉，刘殿元老人在去世前已被迫害致残、不能自理一年之久，但是，沈阳监狱拒绝让老人出狱就医，终将老人迫害致死。目前老人的遗体仍被停放在沈阳殡仪馆。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/87.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/87.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李凤兰：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃白银市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁，原是甘肃省白银市平川区财政局职工。一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共恶党疯狂迫害法轮功，其屡遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，李凤岚被警察叫去白银法院，当晚被关押到白银看守所，随即遭逮捕。后李凤兰女士被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被关押到兰州女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李凤兰乳腺癌细胞都已经扩散，平川区公安局仍不许她保外就医。直到<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，李凤兰家属请了律师，才从监狱接回她。当时的李风兰已经被监狱迫害得奄奄一息，不吃不喝，被直接住进医院，只能在医院打点营养液维持生命，最后医院也不要了，她丈夫无奈把她接回家。没几天，李风兰于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日早上含冤离世。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/1869.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁。而在入狱前，她还是很健康的。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/74.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159764229;"><a name="_Hlk162484044"></a><a name="_Hlk162567084"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162484044;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">张岳兵、雷凤春</span></span></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159764229;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162484044;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159764229;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162484044;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159764229;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162484044;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张岳兵</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159764229;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159764229;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省南通市如皋市人，南通市如皋市如城街道西郊居九组<span lang="EN-US">70</span>号公民，维权公民，公益举报人，中国在押维权人士。早年，曾因其房屋遭政府强拆而被迫上访维权，后在上访过程中逐渐成长为维权公民，并开始致力于关注公益维权事业；自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，曾因举报江苏省如皋市公交违规收费事宜，而如皋市政府和相关部门却一直并未履行法定职责查处和纠正这一违法行为，故而随后其又举报了多个公共场所长期违反消防法占用消防疏散信道经营等违法事项；尽管其举报意图旨在为了社会公益，但地方当局及职能部门却为了自身的集团利益，无视其举报的相关问题，公然失职渎职，维护违反消防法、占用消防车信道和疏散信道等现象，甚至层层谎报，拒不整改、消除障碍及依法查处问题所在；由于如皋市当局对其举报多年的违法事实不予理会也不立案查处，因而为了掩盖政府部门的不作为和乱作为（即几次出现谎报现象），遂长期高薪雇佣多个保安非法限制其人身自由，并将其住所用钢材焊死，非法安装监视器，对其全天候的拍照与跟踪；其虽多次报警但无果；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其因担心电瓶车长久不充电耗损电瓶（因正被长期软禁中），故而到车库欲给电瓶车充电，但竟被监控者跟着，一脚踹开车库门，将其殴打致伤；其即刻电话报警，不料如皋市警方反将其带走，被莫名处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转为刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被如皋市检察院以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案被地方检察院起诉并移交到江苏省南通市如皋市法院；据悉，其律师认为其不构成寻衅滋事罪，已向检察院提交不起诉意见书。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日江苏南通如皋市维权人士张岳兵涉嫌寻衅滋事案宣判，其一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。被羁押于江苏省如皋市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。出狱不到一个星期，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日再次被刑事拘留，因反抗维稳人员对其限制自由，发生冲突，被控故意伤害罪。现在被羁押江苏省如皋市看守所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159764229;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/110.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁沈阳维权人士，男，原是政府体制内人士。因举报领导徇私舞弊、弄虚作假，被领导陷害开除公职，自此开始上访维权。雷凤春从<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年开始，雷凤春积极参与营救被关黑监狱访民、现场声援受迫害访民的庭审、参加在京访民纪念“<span lang="EN-US">9</span>•<span lang="EN-US">18</span>”声讨官僚腐败等活动，屡次遭到当局的打压和迫害，多次被拘留、非法软禁。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年初，雷凤春因到国家信访局多次登记，被沈阳市地方政府强行将他从北京截访回沈阳。回到当地后，沈阳市公安局铁西分局立即于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”将雷凤春刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，雷凤春被沈阳市铁西区检察院批准逮捕。雷凤春被羁押在沈阳市铁西区看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/blog-post_10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">3</span>月，郝京明在重庆九龙坡区石桥铺给民众宣讲法轮功时，被抓捕，关押在沙坪坝白鹤岭看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，郝京明被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，在永川监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，郝京明刑满出狱，回到老家山东青岛平度凤台街道办事处东郝家疃村照顾母亲。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日郝京明在老家山东青岛平度市被警察抓捕、被关押到平度市看守所。随即遭刑事拘留、后被批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，郝京明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">贵阳市法轮功学员，女，生于<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年，家住贵阳市小河经济技术开发区王武村。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，张菊红开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日早上，小河区三江派出所、小河区公安分局警察，闯进张菊红的家，将其抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，张菊红被送往特殊人员过渡隔离点隔离。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被官屯派出所警察抓捕、抄家；六月初被保外就医，后被构陷到检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日其被山东省聊城市冠县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万八千元。其不服上诉，聊城市中级法院二审维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。许恒奎目前关押在山东省监狱服刑。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省德惠市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，从事个体经营。一九九九年六月，他开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共当局疯狂迫害法轮功后，郑玉明因坚持修炼法轮功，曾三次被绑架，两次被劳教，多次遭骚扰迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，德惠市公安局达家沟派出所警察闯到郑玉明的鞋店，实施抓捕、抄家，并将郑玉明夫妇全部带走。警察抢走电脑、打印机、大法书籍等私人财物。后郑玉明被关押到德惠市看守所，他的妻子被放回。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬获悉，郑玉明在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他已被转监到吉林监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/7_28.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王宗尧：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">英文名：<span lang="EN-US">Gregory Wong Chung-yiu</span>，生于<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，香港男演员，杜汶泽喱骚旗下艺人。王宗尧自小家住清水湾半岛龙虾湾，母亲是家庭主妇，父亲经营餐饮、玩具、建村屋等生意，让王宗尧小时候在富裕环境下成长。王宗尧曾就读圣类斯中学（小学部）和圣若瑟小学，毕业于圣方济各英文小学。其后入读传统名校英华书院，中四后往英国留学，曾入读伦敦帝国学院修读关于改变物料的科目，，次年转校到伦敦大学学院修读经济统计学。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，他拍了一部中港台合拍的电视剧《花之恋》；同年，王宗尧在台湾留了六年后回港发展，接拍香港剧集《胜者为王<span lang="EN-US">IV</span>争霸》。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，王宗尧到北京接拍《滚滚红尘》；后来他签约加入了中国<span lang="EN-US">3D</span>数码娱乐。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，占中运动期间，王宗尧全副装备现身龙和道为市民打气。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，因涉嫌在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日占领立法会大楼，被警方以串谋刑事毁坏和进入或逗留会议厅范围罪名拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被改控暴动罪，最高刑期由三个月增至十年，他在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>发文强调「没有暴徒，只有暴政」，指这只是制造恐慌，又勉励香港人勿忘初衷，呼吁「大家不用太担心我」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，宣布签约成为艺人杜汶泽旗下收费平台「哩骚」的首位包薪合约艺人。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日中共操控下的香港特区法院就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“反送中”示威期间发生的“占领立法会暴动案”判刑，王宗尧等<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名示威者暴动罪成立，被判监<span lang="EN-US">4.5</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月不等，其中王宗尧被裁定暴动罪成立，被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/62.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/62.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙淑云：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江哈尔滨市七旬法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，早年修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共疯狂迫害法轮功以来，孙淑云先后曾被非法关押十余次。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月因宣讲法轮功被警方抓捕抄家，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，她被哈尔滨市呼兰区光明派出所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，孙淑云被呼兰区公安局国保大队警察抓捕。随即孙淑云被哈尔滨市道外区检察院批捕。孙淑云被非法关押在哈尔滨第二看守所（鸭子圈看守所）。在第二看守所，她拒绝坐板，拒穿囚服，坚持打坐炼功，以年逾七旬之躯绝食抗议。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在哈尔滨市道外区法院遭开庭，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被转监到黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/6.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">长春市法轮功学员，原籍延边州图们市，女。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，她在长春市绿园区租住处被长春市公安局和二道区分局国保大队警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初获悉，刘晓华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，已被劫入吉林省女子监狱。家属得知消息前往监狱探视，监狱没让见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日中共操控下的香港特区西九龙裁判法院就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“反送中”示威期间发生的“占领立法会暴动案”判刑，邹家成等<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名示威者暴动罪成立，被判监<span
