style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: bold;">山西省忻州市忻府区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，原在忻府区政府工作。常海花因坚持法轮信仰，曾遭中共人员绑架、判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曾被抓捕，并判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。常海花女士<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月份被转监到山西省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年间就读华英中学，在校时曾是该校学生会会长。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年度出任香港大学学生会会长，亦是首名任内表明支持香港独立的香港大学学生会会长。会长任期内被香港政府委任为防止学生自杀委员会委员，为会中唯一的学生成员。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日中共操控下的香港特区西九龙裁判法院就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“反送中”示威期间发生的“占领立法会暴动案”判刑，孙晓岚等<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名示威者暴动罪成立，被判监<span lang="EN-US">4.5</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月不等，其中孙晓岚被裁定暴动罪成立，被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。孙晓岚在其亲自陈词称：“在政权眼中，（我们的）真正罪名是对民主、自由、人权的追求。”</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省烟台市龙口市法轮功学员，女。葛丽娟于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被抓捕，关押在烟台看守所，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，并于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日遭龙口法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，葛丽娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年春节前已被被转监到济南女子监狱，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New bold;">黑龙江省大兴安岭地区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁，家住大兴安岭地区松岭区古源镇。一九九六年五月她开始修炼法轮功。中共迫害法轮功后，郝玉红屡遭迫害。郝玉红因通过网络宣传法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被加格达奇区公安局警察抄家、抓捕，她被关押在加格达奇看守所。之后，郝玉红被加格达奇区公安局警察、检察院和法院暗箱操作构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬，郝玉红被加格达奇法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，她被转监到黑龙江省哈尔滨女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">20288</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/46_13.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/46_13.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">14/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘颕匡：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">英语：<span lang="EN-US">Ventus LAU Wing-hong</span>，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日生，香港本土民主派人士，曾就读顺德联谊总会梁銶琚中学、香港中文大学善衡书院中国语言及文学系。在校期间曾任香港中文大学善衡书院学生会代表会主席，而且创立本土派学生组织中大本土学社。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日因被指控早前参与立法会激进民主派初选涉嫌违犯国安法而被捕，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底被拒保释一直还押至今。刘颕匡于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初应中学老师、新同盟谭凯邦的邀请下，加入新民主同盟，担任沙田博康的地区主任，自此步入政圈。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年初，当时作为中大本土学社召集人的刘颕匡支持中大学生会退出学联，与新同盟「支持学联，反对退联」的立场有所分歧，与范国威就退联及光复行动立场分歧而退党。退出新民主同盟后，刘颕匡创立政治组织沙田小区网络，其成员黄学礼（当时<span lang="EN-US">22</span>岁）于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年区议会选举胜出，成为应届最年轻当选区议员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘颕匡代表小区网络联盟亲笔填写及签署，承诺全力支持及参与由民主动力的九龙西及新界东民主派初选。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，新界东选区选举主任陈婉雯通知刘颕匡他的参选提名「无效」，通知书上声称，刘在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年时，曾在面书上表示支持香港独立；对刘于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在其面书指「基于政治现实」，已不再支持香港独立，陈主观地认定刘「实际上是承认了（至少在此陈述之前）他一直支持香港独立」，并以此非法地剥夺刘的参选权。其后，刘颕匡于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月向高等法院提出选举呈请，挑战选举主任的裁定。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月中，高等法院裁定刘颕匡的选举呈请胜诉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，刘颕匡在家中被警方拘捕，因涉嫌于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日进入立法会，触犯《立法会<span lang="EN-US">(</span>权力及特权<span lang="EN-US">)</span>条例》，于同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被正式落案起诉「进入或逗留在会议厅范围」，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在东区裁判法院提堂。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘颕匡被改控较重的暴动罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，刘透过律师表示，宣布民间集会团队正式解散。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日中共操控下的香港特区西九龙裁判法院就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“反送中”示威期间发生的“占领立法会暴动案”判刑，刘颕匡等<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名示威者暴动罪成立，被判监<span lang="EN-US">4.5</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月不等，其中刘颕匡被裁定暴动罪成立，被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广东揭阳市榕城区东山法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，黄惠君因在榕城区东山街路边贴法轮功资料被榕城分局东兴派出所抓捕，当晚被抄家。次日，黄惠君被刑事拘留，关押至揭阳市看守所。后遭批捕、起诉。后遭揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其被关押至广东女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><a name="_Hlk162481481"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16/</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162481481;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省日照市法轮功学员，男，山东省日照市五莲县叩官镇闫家庄村村民。其妻子马瑞梅女士也是法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日早晨<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点左右，由闫家庄村书记夏京德带路，日照市东港区公安局、东港分局泰安路派出所、五莲县公安局及叩官镇派出所<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多名警察开车闯到丁元德夫妇的茶叶地里，将正在采茶的丁元德夫妇抓捕，随后到他们家中抄家。马瑞梅被单独铐在一辆车中，恰在此时其在德国旅居的儿子给她打来电话。电话接通后，当马瑞梅告知自己被抓，并被戴上手铐时，电话就被警察强行挂断，整个通话时间仅半分钟，此后其子再也无法联系到父母。丁元德、马瑞梅夫妇被劫持到东港区公安分局接受非法审讯，随后被非法关押在东港区小海派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，马瑞梅被关押<span lang="EN-US">12</span>天后被释放，此前马瑞梅因坚持修炼法轮功，曾被非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，在山东省第一女子劳教所遭受迫害，被释放后一直受监控，电话被监听。丁元德仍在派出所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，丁元德被正式批捕。后东港区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底，中共当局对丁元德进行了一场走过场的审判。家人没有收到任何关于审判的官方消息，家属在<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日才得知“审判”结果。五莲县法院判处丁元德<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，并要他缴纳一万五千元人民币罚款，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。其不服一审判决，依法上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日山东省日照市中级法院二审，驳回丁元德的上诉，维持原判。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余发全：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">四川乐山市犍为县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，男，早年修炼法轮功，自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害发了个后，其被两次劳教，一次判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。前后坐牢<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚上，犍为县公安警察四人、社区工作人员二人，闯进法轮功学员余发全（男）、范惠英（女、<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、王玉富（女、<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁）三人家，在余发全住处抄走很多法轮功书籍及打印机、私人笔记本电脑等私人物品。三人被绑架到犍为县公安局，关押近二十四小时，才放回家。余发全、范惠英、王玉富三位法轮功学员都被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，犍为县法院开庭，余发全被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、处罚金五千元；余发全上诉，被中级法院非法维持原判，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午被逮捕收监，关押地点不详。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在长春市被长春市公安局二道分局国保大队警察抓捕，关押到长春市苇子沟拘留所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬获悉：吕永珍被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，目前她被关押在长春市监管中心。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span bold;">京市海淀区四季青乡法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮大法后，杨顺梅因坚持法轮功信仰，坚持给民众宣传法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被劳教，于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年三次非法判刑，总计判刑入狱十二年半。因宣讲法轮功，杨顺梅于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被闯入家中的警察抓捕、抄家，关押在海淀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年，她被海淀中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。杨顺梅现被关押在北京大兴女子监狱服刑。狱方不让家属探视，只让存一点钱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b lang="EN-US">9</span>日，焦麟惠在现住地山东省烟台市下辖的龙口市的家中，被龙口市被龙口市公安局东江派出所警察撬门入室抓捕，关押在烟台看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，焦麟惠被构陷到龙口市检察院，<span name="_Hlk162481284">程海军、朱成芝</a>夫妇，并抄家。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午，凌海市法院判处程海军有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span bold;">又名丁发栋，宁夏银川市法轮功学员丁乾，男，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，现年六十三岁。原系宁夏青铜峡市一所中学的优秀教师，还是宁夏优秀键盘手，他的音乐作品在全国首届中音杯获奖。早年修炼法轮功，一九九九年“七·二零”法轮功遭迫害后，丁乾曾四次被中共非法劳教，曾遭受过关禁闭、坐老虎凳、毒打等酷刑折磨，身陷囹圄逾八年。丁乾<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被青铜峡市公安局警察抓捕，关押在吴忠市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号，丁乾被批捕，后遭起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，其已被吴忠市利通区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金五千元，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月下旬被转监到宁夏石嘴山监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。</span></span></span><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/03/16_23.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162505707;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在辽宁省营口市下辖的盖州市的家中被盖州市公安局国保大队、太阳升派出所警察抓捕，关押在营口看守所。随即遭刑事拘留，后被批捕、起诉。在狱中遭虐待，其曾绝食抗议。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬获悉：董丽萍被营口市站前区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，锦州市北镇市大屯乡派出所警察以发放法轮功资料为由，抓捕了法轮功学员程海军、朱成芝夫妇，并抄家。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午，凌海市法院判处丈夫程海军有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。朱成芝刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span
